  \NormalTok{of <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{knitr::opts_knit$}\KeywordTok{get}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'out.format'}\NormalTok{)}
  \NormalTok{if (of ==}\StringTok{ 'markdown'}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \NormalTok{of <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{knitr::opts_knit$}\KeywordTok{get}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'rmarkdown.pandoc.to'}\NormalTok{)}
    \NormalTok{if (}\KeywordTok{is.null}\NormalTok{(of)) \{}
      \NormalTok{of <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{rmarkdown::}\KeywordTok{default_output_format}\NormalTok{(knitr::}\KeywordTok{current_input}\NormalTok{())}
      \NormalTok{of <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{of$name}
      \NormalTok{of <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'_.*'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{''}\NormalTok{, of)}
      \NormalTok{if (of %in%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'ioslides'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{'revealjs'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{'slidy'}\NormalTok{)) of <-}\StringTok{ 'html'}
    \NormalTok{\}}
  \NormalTok{\}}
  \NormalTok{if (of ==}\StringTok{ 'pdf'}\NormalTok{) of <-}\StringTok{ 'latex'}
  \NormalTok{of}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\FloatBarrier
\# Basic usage

\subsection{Creating a huxtable}\label{creating-a-huxtable}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ht_orig <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{huxtable}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{a =} \KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'Parsley'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{'Sage'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{'Rosemary'}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{'Thyme'}\NormalTok{), }\DataTypeTok{b =} \DecValTok{10} \NormalTok{^}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{)) }
\KeywordTok{width}\NormalTok{(ht_orig) <-}\StringTok{ }\FloatTok{0.25}
\NormalTok{ht_orig <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{set_all_borders}\NormalTok{(ht_orig, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(ht_orig), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\KeywordTok{ncol}\NormalTok{(ht_orig), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{ht_orig}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Borders}\label{borders}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ht <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{ht_orig}
\NormalTok{ht <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{set_all_borders}\NormalTok{(ht, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{:}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\KeywordTok{top_border}\NormalTok{(ht) <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\KeywordTok{bottom_border}\NormalTok{(ht)[}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{,] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2} 
\NormalTok{ht}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Row span}\label{row-span}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ht <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{ht_orig}
\NormalTok{ht[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ 'A rather long block of text'}
\KeywordTok{background_color}\NormalTok{(ht)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ 'green'}
\KeywordTok{rowspan}\NormalTok{(ht)[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] <-}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{2}
\NormalTok{ht   }
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{table}[h]
\begin{centering}\begin{tabularx}{0.25\textwidth}{p{0.125\textwidth} p{0.125\textwidth}}

\hhline{>{\arrayrulecolor{black}}|>{\arrayrulecolor[RGB]{0, 255, 0}}->{\arrayrulecolor{black}}|>{\arrayrulecolor{black}}-}
\arrayrulecolor{black}

\FloatBarrier

\section{Advanced features}\label{advanced-features}

\subsection{Printing on screen}\label{printing-on-screen}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{ht <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{ht_orig}
\CommentTok{# Basic data:}
\KeywordTok{print}\NormalTok{(ht)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
##          a     b
## 1  Parsley 1e+02
## 2     Sage 1e+03
## 3 Rosemary 1e+04
## 4    Thyme 1e+05
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# Pretty print:}
\KeywordTok{print_screen}\NormalTok{(ht)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
##  ------------------------ 
##  | Parsley  | 100.00    | 
##  ------------------------ 
##  | Sage     | 1000.00   | 
##  ------------------------ 
##  | Rosemary | 10000.00  | 
##  ------------------------ 
##  | Thyme    | 100000.00 | 
##  ------------------------
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# Markdown:}
\KeywordTok{print_md}\NormalTok{(ht)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## Parsley                                 100.00                                  
## --------------------------------------- ---------------------------------------
## Sage                                    1000.00                                 
## 
## Rosemary                                10000.00                                
## 
## Thyme                                   100000.00                               
## 
## -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
\end{verbatim}
